        var upDom = document.getElementById('realFlashbox');
        if (!downDom || !upDom) {
            return;
        }

<script>
    function getCookie(name){
          var strcookie = document.cookie;
          var arrcookie = strcookie.split("; ");
          
          for ( var i = 0; i &lt; arrcookie.length; i++) {
            var arr = arrcookie[i].split("=");
            
            if (arr[0] == name){
              return arr[1];
            }
          }
          return "";
    }
    
    function getUserIcon (data) {
        if (data.code === 'A00000') {
            var result = '';
            var suid = getCookie("P00PRU");
            var i, familyList, userInfo;
            
            if (
                data &amp;&amp;
                data.data &amp;&amp;
                data.data.familyInfo &amp;&amp;
                data.data.familyInfo.list
            ) {
                familyList = data.data.familyInfo.list;
                for (i=0; i&lt;familyList.length; i++) {
                    userInfo = familyList[i];
                    if (userInfo.suid === suid) {
                      result = userInfo.icon;
                      break;
                    }
                }
            } else {
                result = data.data.userInfo.icon;
            }
            result = result.replace('http:', '');
        }
        if (!result) {
            if ("$pageName" === 'vip') {
                result = "//www.iqiyipic.com/common/fix/site-v4/header-userImg-default-gold.png";
            } else {
                result = "//www.iqiyipic.com/common/fix/site-v4/header-userImg-default-green.png";
            }
        }
            
        return result;
    }
    function updateUserIcon () {
        var userIconDom = document.querySelector("#J-userIcon");
        var script = document.createElement('script');
        var callbackName = 'updateUserIconCallback';
        var oHead = document.head || document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0];
        var userIcon;
        
        document.domain = "iqiyi.com";
        oHead.insertBefore(script, null);
        window[callbackName] = function (data) {
            setTimeout(function() {
                oHead.removeChild(script);    
            }, 10);
            
            window[callbackName] = null;
            window.pageInfo = window.pageInfo || {};
            userIcon = getUserIcon(data);
            userIconDom.src = userIcon;
            window.pageInfo.userIcon = userIcon;
        }
        script.src = "//pcw-api.iqiyi.com/passport/user/userinfodetail?callback=" + callbackName;
    }
    updateUserIcon();
</script>
